Financial Statement

NOTES TO ACCOUNTS

1. Notes to accounts

These accounting statements have been presented in compliance with generally accepted accounting principles and
by selecting the Sri Lanka public sector accounting policies endorsed by the public sector accounting standards com-
mittee, preparing accounting estimates in timely and fair manner.

It is assured that measures have been taken to present fair financial statements by designing implementing and main-
taining internal control relevant to the preparation and fair presentation of financial statements that are free from
material misstatement, whether due to fraud or error.

2. Accounting Policies

The accounting reports of the Authority have been presented with mutual interconnection between periods of time
and on historic cost basis in accordance with recognized accounting policies. Adjustments have been made towards
inflationary factors that may affect the financial policies and the accounting reports have been prepared on accrual

basis.

3. Location of the Authority

The Condominium Management Authority is located at the National Housing Development Authority at Sir Chittam-
palam A Gardianer Mawatha, Colombo 02 and carries out regulatory duties in respect of condominium properties
covering the entire island.

4. Legal nature of the Authority

In terms of the powers conferred under the Common Amenities Board (Amendment) Act No. 24 of 2003, it is the
responsibility of the Authority to establish management corporations for the maintenance administration and control
of common elements and Common amenities in condominium properties and to ensure that common facilities are
provided so as to fulfill the needs of stakeholders.

5. Legislation relevant for the administration of operations of the Authority
® Common Amenities Board (Amendment) Law No.10 of 1973
€ CommonAmenities Board Act No. 46 of 1982
® Common Amenities Board (Amendment) Act No 24 of 2003
® Apartment Ownership Act No.11 of 1973
€ Apartment Ownership (Amendment) Act No. 45 of 1982
e Apartment Ownership (Special Provisions) No.04 1999
e Apartment Ownership (Amendment) Act 39 of 2003
6. Fixed assets

The provisions for depreciation for fixed assets are calculated by using straight line basis from the date of purchase to
the date of sale as per the policy of the Authority

e      Motor vehicles                                  -25% 0n Cost
e      Office furniture                                 -20% 0n cost
e      Machinery and equipment                 - 20% on cost
e      Office equipment                              - 20% on cost
e      Buildings                                       - 04% on cost

62


Financial Statement

07. Gratuity

Provisions have been made in the accounts on the basis of the period of service of all employees serving in the
Authority for their gratuity. That value relevant to the year ended 31 December 2017 was Rs. 30,919,215 and it had
been invested as fixed deposits as at 31 December 2017.

08. Stocks

Adjustments have been made in the accounts having computed on the lesser value of the stocks purchase cost and
the net realized value and no profit percentage had been included.

9. Revenue
Profit/loss accounts have been prepared on the basis of gross revenue.
10. Allocations for bad and doubtful debt

Allocations for bad and doubtful debt have been made on outcome on the basis of the age analysis of the debtors
existing as at the end of the year.

e      Years 0 -2         10% 656,085

e      Years 2- 3         20% 1,238,149
      Years 3-4         30%     64,470

e       Years 4-5           50% 3,630,382

      Over 5years 100% 6,930,200
Accordingly, a sum of Rs. 8,519,286 has been allocated in the accounts of the current year for bad and doubtful debt.
11. Contingent liabilities

A case has been filed in the district court of Colombo under case number 53429/MR to recover Rs 807,187 due from
Lanka Net (Pvt) Ltd. As there no contingent liabilities in respect of cases filed by or against the Authority, no allocations
have been made in the accounts for that purpose.

12. Lease loan

The said lease loan had been paid off by June 2017.

13. EPF and ETF in arrears

EPF 7 ETF contributions are paid for the employees of the Authority in terms of the provisions of the Employees
Provident Fund Act and as at 31.12.2017, there had not been any payable arrears.

14. Capital projects

Of Rs. 80,000,000 granted for the renovation of housing schemes in the year 2015, action had been taken to return Rs.
32,659,484 to the Ministry on 16th May 2017. Further, out of the money allocated in the year 2015 for the renovation
of roads of 03 housing schemes, Rs. 2,421,000 had been allocated for the remaining work relating to the granting of
title deeds of residents of Tsunami housing schemes. In addition, a Treasury provision amounting to Rs. 10,000,000 was
granted for conducting condominium awareness programmes in the year 2017 and of this amount Rs. 2,309,950 was
spent on purchasing fixed items and Rs. 5,488,585 was deployed in the year 2017 on awareness programmes. Action
had been taken to use the balance of Rs. 2,201,464 in January 2018.



Financial Statement

15. Reserves

Revaluation reserves -Rs. 22,308,765

General reserves        - Rs. 1,350,000
Capital reserves         - RS. 2,262,663
Total reserves            - Rs. 25,921,428

The above reserves to the value of Rs 25,921,428 include Rs. 22,308,765 from the revaluation of fixed assets in the year
2008 and a capital transfer of Rs. 2,262,663.28 carried forward to the accounts of this Authority from its predecessor,

the Common Amenities Board.

16. Bonus shares

In pursuance of approval referred to by Ministry of Public Administration, Housing and Construction dated 12.01.1984,
5000 shares of Rs 100 were obtained from the Housing Development Finance Corporation on 19.01.1984.

A bonus share issue of 25,000 shares in respect of the value of the said shares was issued on 29.06.2000. Accordingly,
action has been taken to disclose in the accounts an investment of Rs. 3,000,000 for 30,000 shares of Rs. 100 each of
the HDFC in possession of this Authority.

17. Income Tax

Provisions have been allocated in accounts for the payment of Rs. 25,990,927 as income tax on the basis of the profit
of Rs. 124,375,570 for the said year as at 31.12.2017.

18. Accounting government grants

In the year 2017 too, the Treasury had allocated Rs. 10,000,000 for creatingawareness amongst partners ofcondominium
properties under the ‘Nagamu Purawara' project and of that amount Rs. 7,798,535 had been spent in the current year.
Similarly, action had been taken to include a sum of Rs 119,081 for the depreciation of fixed assets purchased for the
said project in the project expenditure.

19. Allocation for depreciation

Action had been taken to depreciate fixed assets on the basis of percentages given in fixed assets note number 09.
Accordingly, action had been taken to adjust Rs. 7,984,344 as annual depreciation value to the profit of the current
year.
